### ğŸ“¦ GoogleAppsLauncher.jsx (composant principal)

```jsx
import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import './GoogleAppsLauncher.css';
import { appsList } from './appsList';
import AppIcon from './AppIcon';

const GoogleAppsLauncher = () => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const ref = useRef();

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleClickOutside = (event) => {
      if (ref.current && !ref.current.contains(event.target)) {
        setIsOpen(false);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
  }, []);

  const filteredApps = appsList.filter(app =>
    app.name.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase())
  );

  return (
    <div className="google-launcher-container" ref={ref}>
      <button className="google-launcher-button" onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}>
        <img src="/icons/grid.svg" alt="Apps" />
      </button>

      {isOpen && (
        <div className="google-launcher-dropdown">
          <input
            type="text"
            className="search-bar"
            placeholder="Rechercher une application..."
            value={search}
            onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
          />
          <div className="apps-grid">
            {filteredApps.map((app, index) => (
              <AppIcon key={index} {...app} />
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default GoogleAppsLauncher;
```

---

### ğŸ§± AppIcon.jsx

```jsx
import React from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

const AppIcon = ({ name, icon, path }) => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  return (
    <div className="app-icon" onClick={() => navigate(path)} title={name}>
      <img src={icon} alt={name} />
      <span>{name}</span>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AppIcon;
```

### ğŸ§± `GoogleAppsLauncher.jsx` â€“ RENDU PROFESSIONNEL PAR CATÃ‰GORIE

```jsx
import { appsList } from "./appsList";
import AppIcon from "./AppIcon";
import "./GoogleAppsLauncher.css";

export default function GoogleAppsLauncher() {
  const groupedApps = appsList.reduce((acc, app) => {
    acc[app.category] = acc[app.category] || [];
    acc[app.category].push(app);
    return acc;
  }, {});

  return (
    <div className="launcher-container">
      <h3>Applications SocialMail</h3>
      <input
        type="text"
        placeholder="Rechercher une application..."
        className="launcher-search"
        onChange={e => {/* ajout recherche dynamique */}}
      />
      {Object.entries(groupedApps).map(([category, apps]) => (
        <div key={category}>
          <h4>{category.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + category.slice(1)}</h4>
          <div className="apps-grid">
            {apps.map(app => (
              <AppIcon
                key={app.name}
                emoji={app.emoji}
                label={app.name}
                onClick={() => window.location.href = app.path}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      ))}
      <div className="launcher-footer">
        {appsList.length} applications disponibles
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## ğŸ”§ SERVICES API

### VMwareService.js
```javascript
class VMwareService {
  constructor() {
    this.baseURL = process.env.REACT_APP_VMWARE_API_URL;
    this.session = null;
  }

  async authenticate(credentials) {
    const response = await axios.post(`${this.baseURL}/rest/com/vmware/cis/session`, {}, {
      auth: credentials
    });
    this.session = response.data.value;
    return this.session;
  }

  async getVMs(filters = {}) {
    const response = await this.apiCall('/rest/vcenter/vm', { params: filters });
    const vms = response.data.value;
    return Promise.all(vms.map(vm => this.getVMDetails(vm.vm)));
  }

  async getVMDetails(vmId) {
    const [summary, power, guest] = await Promise.all([
      this.apiCall(`/rest/vcenter/vm/${vmId}`),
      this.apiCall(`/rest/vcenter/vm/${vmId}/power`),
      this.apiCall(`/rest/vcenter/vm/${vmId}/guest/identity`)
    ]);

    return {
      id: vmId,
      ...summary.data.value,
      powerState: power.data.value.state,
      guestOS: guest.data.value
    };
  }

  async executeVmAction(vmId, action, params = {}) {
    const actionMap = {
      start: `POST /rest/vcenter/vm/${vmId}/power/start`,
      stop: `POST /rest/vcenter/vm/${vmId}/power/stop`,
      restart: `POST /rest/vcenter/vm/${vmId}/power/reset`
    };
    
    const [method, path] = actionMap[action].split(' ');
    return this.apiCall(path, { method, data: params });
  }

  async createSnapshot(vmId, name, description) {
    return this.apiCall(`/rest/vcenter/vm/${vmId}/guest/filesystem/directories`, {
      method: 'POST',
      data: { name, description, memory: false, quiesce: true }
    });
  }
}

export default new VMwareService();
```

### Hook useVMware
```javascript
const useVMware = () => {
  const [vms, setVms] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const [selectedVms, setSelectedVms] = useState([]);

  const loadVMs = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      setLoading(true);
      const data = await VMwareService.getVMs();
      setVms(data);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  const executeAction = useCallback(async (vmId, action) => {
    await VMwareService.executeVmAction(vmId, action);
    setTimeout(loadVMs, 1000);
  }, [loadVMs]);

  useEffect(() => { loadVMs(); }, [loadVMs]);

  return { vms, loading, error, selectedVms, setSelectedVms, executeAction };
};
```

## ğŸ¨ COMPOSANTS UI

### VMwareModule.jsx
```javascript
import React from 'react';
import InfraModuleLayout from '../InfraModuleLayout';
import VMwareHeaderActions from './VMwareHeaderActions';
import VMwareCard from './VMwareCard';
import { useVMware } from './hooks/useVMware';

const VMwareModule = () => {
  const { vms, loading, error, executeAction } = useVMware();

  if (loading) return <div>Chargement...</div>;
  if (error) return <div>Erreur: {error.message}</div>;

  return (
    <InfraModuleLayout
      title="VMware vSphere"
      icon="ğŸ–¥ï¸"
      headerActions={<VMwareHeaderActions />}
    >
      <div className="vmware-grid">
        {vms.map(vm => (
          <VMwareCard 
            key={vm.id} 
            vm={vm} 
            onAction={executeAction}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
    </InfraModuleLayout>
  );
};

export default VMwareModule;
```

  --vmware-blue: #0072CE;
  --vmware-green: #5FB85F;
  --vmware-orange: #FF9500;
  --vmware-red: #D32F2F;

## ğŸ§ª TESTS

### Tests unitaires
```javascript
import { render, screen, waitFor } from '@testing-library/react';
import VMwareModule from './VMwareModule';
import VMwareService from './VMwareService';

jest.mock('./VMwareService');

describe('VMwareModule', () => {
  test('loads and displays VMs', async () => {
    VMwareService.getVMs.mockResolvedValue([
      { id: 'vm-001', name: 'Test VM', powerState: 'poweredOn' }
    ]);

    render(<VMwareModule />);
    
    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(screen.getByText('Test VM')).toBeInTheDocument();
    });
  });

  test('handles VM power actions', async () => {
    render(<VMwareModule />);
    
    const powerButton = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /power/i });
    fireEvent.click(powerButton);
    
    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(VMwareService.executeVmAction).toHaveBeenCalledWith('vm-001', 'start');
    });
  });
});
```

### ğŸ¯ **Prompt complet â€“ IntÃ©gration du mode sombre/clair pour SocialMail**

> **Act as a senior frontend engineer** with deep experience in React, Tailwind CSS, CSS Variables, and prefers-color-scheme standards. You are tasked with implementing a fully dynamic **light/dark mode system** for a professional email client app called **SocialMail**.
>
> The theme system must:
>
> ### ğŸ”§ Technical Requirements:
>
> * Be **global**, reactive, and **persist user preference** (`localStorage` or `IndexedDB`).
> * Support `prefers-color-scheme` for automatic system-based fallback.
> * Use **CSS variables** (`:root`) for color theming (avoid hardcoded Tailwind classes).
> * Provide a **`ThemeProvider` component** wrapping the app and a `useTheme()` hook.
> * Allow **toggle from any component** via context (`light â†” dark`).
> * Include a **`ThemeSwitcher` button** with icon (sun/moon), accessible via `aria-label`, keyboard, and with smooth transition animations.
> * Add **a class `theme-light` or `theme-dark`** to `<html>` or `<body>` to allow easy Tailwind overrides (`dark:`).
> * Support **custom themes** (e.g., `Professional`, `Modern`, `Colorful`) with predefined palettes.
>
> ### ğŸ¨ Design Guidelines:
>
> * Match UI tone of apps like Gmail, Notion, Slack.

## Solutions techniques

### 1. **VÃ©rifier la structure HTML**
```html

    <!-- Contenu sidebar -->
  </div>
  <div class="main-content">
    <!-- Contenu principal -->
  </div>

```

### 2. **Modifier le CSS pour gÃ©rer la largeur dynamique**
```css

  display: grid;
  grid-template-columns: auto 1fr; /* Quand sidebar visible */
  transition: grid-template-columns 0.3s ease;
}

.layout-container.sidebar-hidden {
  grid-template-columns: 0 1fr; /* Quand sidebar masquÃ©e */
}

  width: 0;
  overflow: hidden;
}

.main-content {
  width: 100%;
  transition: width 0.3s ease;
}
```

### 3. **Alternative avec Flexbox**
```css

  display: flex;
}

  flex: 0 0 250px; /* Largeur fixe de 250px */
  transition: flex 0.3s ease;
}

.sidebar.hidden {
  flex: 0 0 0;
  overflow: hidden;
}

.main-content {
  flex: 1; /* Prend tout l'espace restant */
}
```

  const workspace = slackWorkspaces.find(w => w.domain === 'sogerhwit.dz');
  if (workspace) {
    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, workspace });
  }
  return res.status(200).json({ success: false, workspace: null });
});

// ğŸš€ POST /create-workspace : crÃ©er un nouvel espace

  const data = req.body;

  if (!data.workspaceName || !data.domain || !data.userId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'DonnÃ©es manquantes' });
  }

    id: Date.now().toString(),
    ...data,
    channels: [],
    setupComplete: false
  };

  slackWorkspaces.push(newWorkspace);
  return res.status(201).json({ success: true, workspace: newWorkspace });
});

// ğŸ§± POST /setup-channels : configurer les canaux
router.post('/setup-channels', (req, res) => {
  const { workspaceId, channels } = req.body;

  const workspace = slackWorkspaces.find(w => w.id === workspaceId);
  if (!workspace) {
    return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Workspace non trouvÃ©' });
  }

  workspace.channels = channels || ['gÃ©nÃ©ral', 'projets', 'hydraulique'];
  workspace.setupComplete = true;

  return res.status(200).json({ success: true, channels: workspace.channels });
});

const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const SlackWorkspace = require('../models/SlackWorkspace');

// GET ALL WORKSPACES
exports.getAllWorkspaces = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const workspaces = await SlackWorkspace.find({});
    console.log(`âœ… ${workspaces.length} workspaces trouvÃ©s`);
    
    res.json({
      success: true,
      workspaces: workspaces,
      total: workspaces.length
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ Erreur getAllWorkspaces:', error);
    res.status(500).json({
      success: false,
      error: 'Erreur lors de la rÃ©cupÃ©ration des workspaces'
    });
  }
};

// CREATE WORKSPACE (PROBLÃˆME PRINCIPAL)
exports.createWorkspace = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { name, domain, logo, description, region, sector } = req.body;
    
    if (!name || !domain) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: 'Nom et domaine requis'
      });
    }
    
    // VÃ©rifier si le domaine existe dÃ©jÃ 
    const existingWorkspace = await SlackWorkspace.findOne({ domain });
    if (existingWorkspace) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: 'Ce domaine est dÃ©jÃ  utilisÃ©'
      });
    }
    
    // CrÃ©er le workspace complet
    const newWorkspace = {
      id: uuidv4(),
      name,
      domain,
      logo: logo || 'ğŸ’§',
      description: description || '',
      region: region || 'Tlemcen',
      sector: sector || 'Hydraulique',
      createdAt: new Date(),
      channels: [{
        id: uuidv4(),
        name: 'gÃ©nÃ©ral',
        type: 'public',
        description: 'Canal principal',
        members: []
      }],
      users: [],
      invitations: [],
      stats: {
        totalMembers: 0,
        totalChannels: 1,
        totalMessages: 0
      }
    };
    
    // Sauvegarder en BDD
    const savedWorkspace = await SlackWorkspace.create(newWorkspace);
    console.log('âœ… Workspace crÃ©Ã©:', savedWorkspace.id);
    
    res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      workspace: savedWorkspace,
      message: 'Workspace crÃ©Ã© avec succÃ¨s'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ Erreur createWorkspace:', error);
    res.status(500).json({
      success: false,
      error: 'Erreur lors de la crÃ©ation du workspace'
    });
  }
};

// GET WORKSPACE BY ID
exports.getWorkspaceById = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { id } = req.params;
    const workspace = await SlackWorkspace.findOne({ id });
    
    if (!workspace) {
      return res.status(404).json({
        success: false,
        error: 'Workspace non trouvÃ©'
      });
    }
    
    res.json({
      success: true,
      workspace
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ Erreur getWorkspaceById:', error);
    res.status(500).json({
      success: false,
      error: 'Erreur lors de la rÃ©cupÃ©ration du workspace'
    });
  }
};

// 2. ğŸ¨ FRONTEND - SlackWorkspaceSelector.jsx (CORRIGÃ‰)
// ========================================

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const SlackWorkspaceSelector = ({ 
  onWorkspaceSelect, 
  onCreateNew, 
  setCurrentStep 
}) => {
  const [workspaces, setWorkspaces] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchWorkspaces();
  }, []);

  const fetchWorkspaces = async () => {
    try {
      setLoading(true);
      
      const response = await fetch('/api/socialmail/slack-sogerhwit/workspaces', {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`,
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        }
      });
      
      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
      }
      
      const data = await response.json();
      console.log('âœ… Workspaces rÃ©cupÃ©rÃ©s:', data);
      
      if (data.success) {
        setWorkspaces(data.workspaces || []);
      } else {
        setError(data.error || 'Erreur inconnue');
      }
      
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('âŒ Erreur fetch workspaces:', error);
      setError('Impossible de charger les workspaces');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // ğŸ¯ SÃ‰LECTION D'UN WORKSPACE (CORRECTION PRINCIPALE)
  const handleWorkspaceSelect = (workspace) => {
    console.log('ğŸ¯ Workspace sÃ©lectionnÃ©:', workspace);
    
    if (!workspace || !workspace.id) {
      console.error('âŒ Workspace invalide:', workspace);
      return;
    }
    
    // Appeler la fonction parent
    if (onWorkspaceSelect) {
      onWorkspaceSelect(workspace);
    }
    
    // Changer vers le dashboard
    if (setCurrentStep) {
      setCurrentStep('dashboard');
    }
  };

  if (loading) {
    return <div className="loading">ğŸ”„ Chargement...</div>;
  }

  if (error) {
    return (
      <div className="error">
        <div>âŒ {error}</div>
        <button onClick={fetchWorkspaces}>ğŸ”„ RÃ©essayer</button>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="slack-workspace-selector">
      <h2>ğŸ¢ Choisir un espace de travail</h2>

      <div className="workspace-grid">
        {workspaces.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="no-workspaces">
            <p>Aucun workspace trouvÃ©</p>
            <button onClick={onCreateNew}>
              â• CrÃ©er votre premier espace
            </button>
          </div>
        ) : (
          workspaces.map(workspace => (
            <div 
              key={workspace.id}
              className="workspace-card"
              onClick={() => handleWorkspaceSelect(workspace)}
            >
              <div className="workspace-logo">
                {workspace.logo || 'ğŸ’§'}
              </div>
              <div className="workspace-info">
                <h3>{workspace.name}</h3>
                <p>{workspace.domain}</p>
                <p>{workspace.region}</p>
                <div className="workspace-stats">
                  <span>ğŸ‘¥ {workspace.stats?.totalMembers || 0}</span>
                  <span>ğŸ“¢ {workspace.stats?.totalChannels || 0}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))
        )}
      </div>

      <button onClick={onCreateNew}>
        â• CrÃ©er un nouvel espace de travail
      </button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default SlackWorkspaceSelector;

    // Mettre Ã  jour tous les Ã©tats
    setSelectedWorkspace(workspace);
    setWorkspaceData(workspace);
    setCurrentStep('dashboard');
    
    console.log('âœ… Workspace sÃ©lectionnÃ© et Ã©tats mis Ã  jour');
  };

  const handleCreateNew = () => {
    console.log('ğŸ¯ CrÃ©ation d\'un nouveau workspace');
    setCurrentStep('creator');
  };

  const handleWorkspaceCreated = (newWorkspace) => {
    console.log('ğŸ¯ Nouveau workspace crÃ©Ã©:', newWorkspace);
    setSelectedWorkspace(newWorkspace);
    setWorkspaceData(newWorkspace);
    setCurrentStep('onboarding');
  };

  const handleBackToSelector = () => {
    setCurrentStep('selector');
    setSelectedWorkspace(null);
    setWorkspaceData(null);
  };

  return (
    <div className="slack-sogerhwit">
      <div className="slack-header">
        <h1>ğŸ’§ Slack SOGERHWIT</h1>
        {selectedWorkspace && (
          <div className="current-workspace">
            <span>{selectedWorkspace.logo} {selectedWorkspace.name}</span>
            <button onClick={handleBackToSelector}>ğŸ”„ Changer</button>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="slack-content">
        {currentStep === 'selector' && (
          <SlackWorkspaceSelector
            onWorkspaceSelect={handleWorkspaceSelect}
            onCreateNew={handleCreateNew}
            setCurrentStep={setCurrentStep}
          />
        )}

        {currentStep === 'creator' && (
          <SlackWorkspaceCreator
            onWorkspaceCreated={handleWorkspaceCreated}
            onBack={handleBackToSelector}
            setCurrentStep={setCurrentStep}
          />
        )}

        {currentStep === 'onboarding' && (
          <div className="onboarding-section">
            <h2>ğŸš€ Configuration de {selectedWorkspace?.name}</h2>
            <p>Configurez vos canaux, invitez des utilisateurs...</p>
            <button onClick={() => setCurrentStep('dashboard')}>
              Continuer vers le dashboard
            </button>
          </div>
        )}

        {currentStep === 'dashboard' && selectedWorkspace && (
          <div className="dashboard-section">
            <h2>ğŸ“Š Dashboard - {selectedWorkspace.name}</h2>
            <div className="dashboard-content">
              <div className="workspace-info">
                <h3>Informations</h3>
                <p>Domaine: {selectedWorkspace.domain}</p>
                <p>RÃ©gion: {selectedWorkspace.region}</p>
                <p>Secteur: {selectedWorkspace.sector}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="workspace-stats">
                <h3>Statistiques</h3>
                <p>ğŸ‘¥ Membres: {selectedWorkspace.stats?.totalMembers || 0}</p>
                <p>ğŸ“¢ Canaux: {selectedWorkspace.stats?.totalChannels || 0}</p>
                <p>ğŸ’¬ Messages: {selectedWorkspace.stats?.totalMessages || 0}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const mongoose = require('mongoose');

const SlackWorkspaceSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
  id: { type: String, required: true, unique: true },
  name: { type: String, required: true },
  domain: { type: String, required: true, unique: true },
  logo: { type: String, default: 'ğŸ’§' },
  description: String,
  region: String,
  sector: String,
  createdAt: { type: Date, default: Date.now },
  channels: [{
    id: String,
    name: String,
    type: String,
    description: String,
    members: [String]
  }],
  users: [{
    id: String,
    email: String,
    name: String,
    role: String,
    status: String
  }],
  invitations: [{
    email: String,
    role: String,
    status: String,
    token: String,
    sentAt: Date
  }],
  stats: {
    totalMembers: { type: Number, default: 0 },
    totalChannels: { type: Number, default: 1 },
    totalMessages: { type: Number, default: 0 }
  }
});

module.exports = mongoose.model('SlackWorkspace', SlackWorkspaceSchema);

### 2. ğŸ’¬ MESSAGERIE TEMPS RÃ‰EL AVEC SOCKET.IO

#### Architecture WebSocket
```javascript
// Server-side Socket.io structure
io.on('connection', (socket) => {
  // Authentication
  socket.on('authenticate', (token) => {
    // JWT verification
    // Join user-specific room
  });

  // Workspace management
  socket.on('join-workspace', (workspaceId) => {
    socket.join(`workspace-${workspaceId}`);
  });

  // Channel management
  socket.on('join-channel', (channelId) => {
    socket.join(`channel-${channelId}`);
    socket.broadcast.to(`channel-${channelId}`).emit('user-joined');
  });

  // Message handling
  socket.on('send-message', async (data) => {
    // Validate & persist message
    // Emit to channel members
    // Handle mentions & notifications
  });

  // Typing indicators
  socket.on('typing-start', (channelId) => {
    socket.broadcast.to(`channel-${channelId}`).emit('user-typing');
  });

  // Presence system
  socket.on('status-change', (status) => {
    // Update user status
    // Broadcast to workspace members
  });
});
```

#### Frontend React Integration
```javascript
// Socket Context Provider
const SocketContext = createContext();

// Custom hooks
const useSocket = () => useContext(SocketContext);
const useMessages = (channelId) => {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);
  const socket = useSocket();
  
  useEffect(() => {
    socket.on('new-message', (message) => {
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, message]);
    });
    
    return () => socket.off('new-message');
  }, [channelId]);
  
  return { messages, sendMessage };
};
```

### 3. ğŸ”” SYSTÃˆME DE NOTIFICATIONS AVANCÃ‰

#### Architecture Multi-Canal
```javascript
// Notification Service
class NotificationService {
  async sendNotification(userId, notification) {
    const user = await User.findById(userId);
    
    // In-app notification
    io.to(`user-${userId}`).emit('notification', notification);
    
    // Push notification
    if (user.pushSubscription) {
      await webpush.sendNotification(user.pushSubscription, notification);
    }
    
    // Email notification (batch)
    await emailQueue.add('send-notification-email', {
      userId,
      notification,
      delay: 60000 // 1 minute delay for batching
    });
  }
}
```

#### Types de notifications
- **Mentions directes** (@username)
- **Messages privÃ©s**
- **Invitations workspace**
- **RÃ©ponses aux threads**
- **Nouveaux canaux**
- **Statuts utilisateurs**

- **Heures de silence** (Do Not Disturb)

#### Service Worker avancÃ©
```javascript
// sw.js
const CACHE_NAME = 'sogerhwit-v1';
const urlsToCache = [
  '/',
  '/static/js/bundle.js',
  '/static/css/main.css',
  '/offline.html'
];

// Strategy: Cache First pour les assets, Network First pour les donnÃ©es
self.addEventListener('fetch', (event) => {
  if (event.request.url.includes('/api/')) {
    // Network First pour les APIs
    event.respondWith(networkFirst(event.request));
  } else {
    // Cache First pour les assets
    event.respondWith(cacheFirst(event.request));
  }
});

// Background sync pour les messages hors ligne
self.addEventListener('sync', (event) => {
  if (event.tag === 'send-message') {
    event.waitUntil(sendPendingMessages());
  }
});
```

#### Backend Optimizations
```javascript
// Redis caching
const redis = require('redis');
const client = redis.createClient();

// Cache des messages rÃ©cents
const getCachedMessages = async (channelId) => {
  const cached = await client.get(`messages:${channelId}`);
  if (cached) return JSON.parse(cached);
  
  const messages = await Message.find({ channelId })
    .sort({ createdAt: -1 })
    .limit(50)
    .populate('sender', 'username avatar');
    
  await client.setex(`messages:${channelId}`, 300, JSON.stringify(messages));
  return messages;
};

// Rate limiting
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const messageLimit = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 60 * 1000, // 1 minute
  max: 60, // 60 messages per minute
  message: 'Trop de messages envoyÃ©s'
});

// Database connection pooling
const mongoose = require('mongoose');
mongoose.connect(process.env.MONGODB_URI, {
  maxPoolSize: 10,
  serverSelectionTimeoutMS: 5000,
  socketTimeoutMS: 45000,
});
```

## ğŸ” SÃ‰CURITÃ‰ & CONTRÃ”LES AVANCÃ‰S

### Authentication & Authorization
```javascript
// JWT avec refresh tokens
const generateTokens = (user) => {
  const accessToken = jwt.sign(
    { userId: user._id, email: user.email },
    process.env.JWT_SECRET,
    { expiresIn: '15m' }
  );
  
  const refreshToken = jwt.sign(
    { userId: user._id },
    process.env.REFRESH_SECRET,
    { expiresIn: '7d' }
  );
  
  return { accessToken, refreshToken };
};

// Middleware d'autorisation workspace
const requireWorkspaceAccess = (requiredRole = 'member') => {
  return async (req, res, next) => {
    const { workspaceId } = req.params;
    const userId = req.user.userId;
    
    const membership = await Workspace.findOne({
      _id: workspaceId,
      'members.userId': userId
    }, {
      'members.$': 1
    });
    
    if (!membership || !hasPermission(membership.members[0].role, requiredRole)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'AccÃ¨s interdit' });
    }
    
    next();
  };
};
```

### Data Validation & Sanitization
```javascript
// Validation avec Joi
const messageSchema = Joi.object({
  content: Joi.string().min(1).max(4000).required(),
  channelId: Joi.string().pattern(/^[0-9a-fA-F]{24}$/).required(),
  mentions: Joi.array().items(Joi.string().pattern(/^[0-9a-fA-F]{24}$/)),
  attachments: Joi.array().items(Joi.object({
    url: Joi.string().uri(),
    filename: Joi.string(),
    size: Joi.number().max(10485760) // 10MB max
  }))
});

// Sanitization XSS
const DOMPurify = require('dompurify');
const sanitizeMessage = (content) => {
  return DOMPurify.sanitize(content, {
    ALLOWED_TAGS: ['b', 'i', 'em', 'strong', 'a', 'code', 'pre'],
    ALLOWED_ATTR: ['href']
  });
};
```

### Rate Limiting & Abuse Protection
```javascript
// Rate limiting avancÃ©
const rateLimiter = {
  messages: rateLimit({
    windowMs: 60 * 1000,
    max: 60,
    keyGenerator: (req) => `${req.user.userId}:messages`
  }),
  
  invitations: rateLimit({
    windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hour
    max: 10,
    keyGenerator: (req) => `${req.user.userId}:invitations`
  }),
  
  fileUploads: rateLimit({
    windowMs: 60 * 1000,
    max: 5,
    keyGenerator: (req) => `${req.user.userId}:uploads`
  })
};
```
